-}</a>

<a id="1131" class="Comment">--</a>

<a id="1499" class="Comment">-- Note that for any equivalence (f , e) : X ≃ Y the type  ι (X , s) (Y , t) (f , e) need not to be</a>
<a id="1599" class="Comment">-- a proposition. Indeed this type should correspond to the ways s and t can be identified</a>
<a id="1690" class="Comment">-- as S-structures. This we call a standard notion of structure or SNS.</a>
<a id="1762" class="Comment">-- We will use a different definition, but the two definitions are interchangeable.</a>

<a id="2319" class="Comment">-- Our new definition of standard notion of structure SNS₂ using the ⋆ notation.</a>
<a id="2400" class="Comment">-- This is easier to work with than SNS₁ wrt Glue-types</a>

<a id="4339" class="Comment">-- We can easily go between SNS₃ (which is def. equal to SNS₂) and SNS₄</a>
<a id="4411" class="Comment">-- We should be able to find are more direct version of PathP≃Path for the family (λ i → S (ua f i))</a>
<a id="4512" class="Comment">-- using glue and unglue terms.</a>

class="Function">f⁻</a> <a id="9172" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9173" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#7980" class="Function">f⁺</a> <a id="9176" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#7906" class="Function">p&#39;</a><a id="9178" class="Symbol">))</a>
    <a id="9185" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="9195" class="Comment">-- This is where we need the half-adjoint equivalence property</a>
    <a id="9262" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#9262" class="Function">eq</a> <a id="9265" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9267" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#1383" class="Function">ua-pathToEquiv</a> <a id="9282" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9283" href="Cubical.Foundations.Univalence.html#873" class="Function">ua</a> <a id="9286" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#7484" class="Bound">e</a><a id="9287" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9289" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="9291" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#1057" class="Function">cong</a> <a id="9296" href="Cubical.Foundations.Univalence.html#873" class="Function">ua</a> <a id="9299" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9300" href="Cubical.Foundations.Univalence.html#5991" class="Function">pathToEquiv-ua</a> <a id="9315" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#7484" class="Bound">e</a><a id="9316" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="9322" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#9262" class="Function">eq</a> <a id="9325" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9327" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#893" class="Function">sym</a> <a id="9331" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9332" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#1134" class="Function">uaHAEquiv</a> <a id="9342" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9343" href="Cubical.Foundations.Structure.html#484" class="Function">typ</a> <a id="9347" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#7479" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9348" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9350" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9351" href="Cubical.Foundations.Structure.html#484" class="Function">typ</a> <a id="9355" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#7481" class="Bound">B</a><a id="9356" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9358" class="Symbol">.</a><a id="9359" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#264" class="Field">snd</a> <a id="9363" class="Symbol">.</a><a id="9364" href="Cubical.Foundations.HAEquiv.html#614" class="Field">com</a> <a id="9368" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#7484" class="Bound">e</a><a id="9369" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="9374" class="Comment">-- We then get a term of the type we need</a>

               <a id="9519" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9520" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#7980" class="Function">f⁺</a> <a id="9523" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#7906" class="Function">p&#39;</a><a id="9525" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9527" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9528" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#8185" class="Function">f⁻</a> <a id="9531" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9532" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#7980" class="Function">f⁺</a> <a id="9535" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#7906" class="Function">p&#39;</a><a id="9537" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="10019" class="Comment">-- Now, we want to add axioms (i.e. propositions) to our Structure S that don&#39;t affect the ι.</a>
<a id="10113" class="Comment">-- For this and the remainder of this file we will work with SNS₂</a>
<a id="10179" class="Comment">-- We use a lemma due to Zesen Qian, which can now be found in Foundations.Prelude:</a>
